CSTA 2015 Board of Directors Elections and Proposed Bylaws Changes
Dear CSTA Membership,
The 2015 CSTA Board of Directors Elections will run from April 2, 2015 to May 4,
 2015. In addition to three open positions on the Board, this year's ballot will
 contain two proposed changes to the CSTA Bylaws. Each CSTA member, including institutional
members, should receive an email on April 2 containing a personalized link to the
election ballot. This email will originate from electionbuddy.com [http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?f=001qa7ySU9DasI-1fFK5NwtxT2rtixWlq4IckW9scZ3xIJ49GaFtz78dzG_wtLt7joEibxkQXn75qFctEDhPP4S__L9Piwl16CaOiMNtbBdnDepADUcKm6ARlATG-PUEL7btMsQlDgdnjA7M1b9xbK7GA0THapCf4DtQ0YYO-0tIAQ=&c=HwvptUT04VmHa1wKpsbRoTTpXpBu4xD5y-wWgwsxkUCCyALtyf1v6A==&ch=ao7ys1m3LLAyF-gFos9rFemJctxE6zSVyfYvk8O2_zY14E8pkSymzA==],
our election service provider, so be sure to look for this email and/or whitelist
the sender in your spam filter. If your email address has changed recently, notify
customerservice at csta-hq.org [mailto:customerservice at csta-hq.org] with your correct
address.
The three open Board positions in the 2015 election are:
K-8 Representative (1 position): A classroom teacher who is currently teaching or
promoting computer science at the pre-high school level.
9-12 Representative (1 position): A 9-12 classroom teacher who is currently teaching
computer science at the high school level.
At-Large Representative (1 position): An educator with responsibilities for K-12
 CS education.
The nominees for each of these positions can be viewed here [http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?f=001qa7ySU9DasI-1fFK5NwtxT2rtixWlq4IckW9scZ3xIJ49GaFtz78dzG_wtLt7joEzFRvuQbWMJDeH7Kh8tHhi7uQas8k2DZWS0713If2ZL5YaPTaOZhYMe_ZRQfpQEa7fwJ_HPqH08g-u8ZCQ11YMcEbzpOvyoJH9xbaGRG-KQi4etxGrHe5hTsiYD4XoWi7pS2Nv6sgk7NfFsliYntWN6IvpqkVNSq8XRN8Av7G49JTKBulMjlm_A==&c=HwvptUT04VmHa1wKpsbRoTTpXpBu4xD5y-wWgwsxkUCCyALtyf1v6A==&ch=ao7ys1m3LLAyF-gFos9rFemJctxE6zSVyfYvk8O2_zY14E8pkSymzA==],
along with their personal statements and Q&A responses. In addition, members can
 read nominee blog posts at the CSTA Advocate Blog [http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?f=001qa7ySU9DasI-1fFK5NwtxT2rtixWlq4IckW9scZ3xIJ49GaFtz78d-sGSyYNNeoQykn8k5bRVKNliprYYfT3b1oQj0wnx1IEOHk66g8WGJMIWCcMn4_qr3cPst-J3DKLpzExyZpippSDt2EAzLOA2Eu_HUQ3vceiA8TYKiIf734=&c=HwvptUT04VmHa1wKpsbRoTTpXpBu4xD5y-wWgwsxkUCCyALtyf1v6A==&ch=ao7ys1m3LLAyF-gFos9rFemJctxE6zSVyfYvk8O2_zY14E8pkSymzA==].

To our valued CSTA members,

Our 2015 annual conference is fast-approaching. This year, as you may be aware, 
we're in Grapevine, Texas, and we're excited to have excellent, top-notch speakers
presenting on all things computer science related.

An important role at any event such as ours is that of an inspirational, exciting
keynote speaker. We feel honored to have Randy Pitchford, CEO/President of Gearbox
Software to be our afternoon keynote presenter to close our conference on a high
 point. This is where we need your help! Gearbox has come up with three engaging
 titles for their presentation, and you, our members get to choose which one it 
will be! Which of the following best suites your fancy and gauges the most interest?
Please respond to our poll by Friday, April 17. We'll compile answers and send to
Gearbox so that they can best speak to your interests. See if your suggestion made
the cut and join us for this presentation, and plenty more at our summer conference,
July 12-14 at the Hilton DFW Lakes Executive Conference Center: www.cstaconference.org.
[http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?f=001SCxyBjWcbfbyVpWkIPtpMc3cr2Q-Myqlwpi_VltJJFGwvY-rGeMJXVl-dcEJPuwG-WjXbsYGzB4kzSjGTJUllDHTB1jEZnjMHzw83XZ2xBaGXRwQwrvhMyzwxWE8myWbUIMoy-uIrtRuN4W00cAhJf5OMMPn4yMdeGcue98dgehwT8YOVPBeoA==&c=KmyCmZNt38M3n5UugO-Y4vXrBVxbJ3H5egw0fLgVZQnDCDHdT6NSmg==&ch=12PPU11x2i7jeK_WXjHinN04ZAZ_Y1jV6u1iKa5XOWRz1W80Pd_LQw==]

[http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?f=001SCxyBjWcbfbyVpWkIPtpMc3cr2Q-Myqlwpi_VltJJFGwvY-rGeMJXY7JcCu11xITj6ZES-GT2SPVvXgnQYuX6EiTO9MBakgGzP8sBx3lk0kuo3VzAHqhlQUawikKf_5ueHeTo9sLtVCo9z7JCw4xoCNsJFjJmeJkapum9CDT385s-Uj5jRBi5DqaklvPAV6w&c=KmyCmZNt38M3n5UugO-Y4vXrBVxbJ3H5egw0fLgVZQnDCDHdT6NSmg==&ch=12PPU11x2i7jeK_WXjHinN04ZAZ_Y1jV6u1iKa5XOWRz1W80Pd_LQw==]

 to get the CSTA annual conference off to a festive start. Connect with other CS4HS
alumni and share your latest CS resources over snow cones and nibbles. Space is 
limited so sign up now and don't delay! Please note, This event is open to current
and past CS4HS participants only, and you must be pre-registered as a CSTA 2015 
attendee as well. Don't be discouraged if you are not a current or past CS4HS participant,
there will be
a networking event at the same time, which will be open to all attendees.

Nationwide Open-Enrollment Workshop for Bootstrap!
Philadelphia, PA :: August 5th-7th, 2015

We're thrilled to announce our biggest workshop of the year, held at the University
of Pennsylvania School of Engineering and Applied Science on August 5th-7th. Most
of our workshops are offered through school districts or partner institutions, but
we want to make this PD available for everyone. If you've wanted to attend our PD
in the past, but weren't able to bring Bootstrap to your district, this is your 
chance! We're grateful to Stephanie Weirich and others at Penn for their support,
enabling us to open Bootstrap to educators everywhere. Join teachers from across
 the country, and discover how to bring Boostrap to your classroom, afterschool 
program or summer camp. Registrations are handled on a first-come, first-served 
basis, putting every educator on the same footing - regardless of the size of your
school district. Enrollment is limited, so reserve your seat today! (Fee: $150/person)
Contact: Emmanuel Schanzer, schanzer at bootstrapworld.org [mailto:schanzer at bootstrapworld.org]
Sign up link: bit.ly/bootstrapPA [http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?f=0016VFMAvgNFKiWDOxWi1-bLRVKdLw_ceO-2le4McqsdRaXcIxjNlLYeojnw8PAMidkhvDsbq7WKtzicLN-N6ctzJmZFwMSjAr4NMdzPjoVIbazjgam8ZTqlPHz0xYk2yRQs74cOBfZK9g4Ua8qxKj0KZr0_inD_OVv8L91IJ20q-4=&c=iFcXPgXtY042L6ARXFvZ8pG9HFN2Nykq5UBa3O6iN4ZCaSh6QMfA5w==&ch=V-XBC_RFK83SAaDX_V-c5Ipdq2tccOINZJLVMWCkeZRhefWfu0jGig==]

Hi, just a reminder that you're receiving this email because you have expressed 
an interest in CSTA. Don't forget to add announcements at csta-hq.org to your address
book so we'll be sure to land in your inbox!
Dear CSTA community,
The Computer Science Teachers Association would like to hear what our friends have
to say about the growing concerns regarding computer science in high schools across
the U.S. In an effort to provide research-based information for educators, decision-makers,
and researchers, CSTA conducts regular national surveys of high school computer 
science teachers and disseminates the results of these surveys to the educational
community.
We are looking for feedback from all U.S. computer science teachers, grades 9-12.
Please take a few minutes to complete our brief survey, and we'd be delighted if
 you additionally shared with your colleagues.
Survey link: https://www.surveymonkey.com/s/2015NatHSCS [http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?f=001jDe1eHWTuntGhz98KHQntfJH-GdzK1gTpzCk9ZYmg5zJDS2VIMEyh1OZjvTK5WiI3X0voexmbdTSKocAy2D2sVjEH1s-Rz0JhtkJ2-nbt7pSTIzY_7DpVGQnNWSa0e0c4-byOSwbjizoBhPPFSykYl-zoMzPgSABUEFgJ35PHf7gD-V3v6gPaTXyQknsBoubMKp7GMbRyzo=&c=Of_dV9U5IUq8S-0SYwC734Eus_aVZVylvSO1Li0hkAgJJDepf_bsHw==&ch=PRYLBdYxRoPXAqW4Va85iyFpiAVuiTDiSc_nBBaiUWCUmmhITv-eZg==]
We know your time is valuable, and as a thank you, all entrants received by May 
5 can opt to be included in our drawing for one of five $100 Amazon gift cards. 
We truly appreciate your input on this important matter, and we assure you that 
your opinions will be treated confidentially.
Kind Regards,
Stephanie Hoeppner, CSTA Board and Research Committee Member
Aman Yadav, CSTA Board and Research Committee Member
P.S. This survey will close on May 5, 2015, at 11:59pm HST.

Call for Papers

ICDM '15: The 15th IEEE International Conference on Data Mining
***************************************************************

November 14-17, 2015, Atlantic City, NJ, USA
http://icdm2015.stonybrook.edu/

Important Dates
***************

All deadlines are at 11:59PM Pacific Daylight Time

* Conference dates:                                  Nov 14-17, 2015

The IEEE International Conference on Data Mining series (ICDM) has
established itself as the world's premier research conference in data
mining. It provides an international forum for presentation of
original research results, as well as exchange and dissemination of
innovative, practical development experiences. The conference covers
all aspects of data mining, including algorithms, software and
systems, and applications. ICDM draws researchers and application
developers from a wide range of data mining related areas such as
statistics, machine learning, pattern recognition, databases and data
warehousing, data visualization, knowledge-based systems, and high
performance computing. By promoting novel, high quality research
findings, and innovative solutions to challenging data mining
problems, the conference seeks to continuously advance the
state-of-the-art in data mining.

Topics of Interest
******************

Topics of interest include, but are not limited to:

* Foundations, algorithms, models, and theory of data mining
* Machine learning and statistical methods for data mining
* Mining text, semi-structured, spatio-temporal, streaming, graph,
  web, multimedia data
* Data mining systems and platforms, their efficiency, scalability,
  and privacy
* Data mining in modeling, visualization, personalization, and
  recommendation
* Applications of data mining in all domains including social, web,
  bioinformatics, and finance

Submission Guidelines
*********************

Paper submissions should be limited to a maximum of ten (10) pages, in
the IEEE 2-column format (templates available at
http://www.ieee.org/conferences_events/conferences/publishing/templates.html
),
including the bibliography and any possible appendices. Submissions
longer than 10 pages will be rejected without a review. All
submissions will be triple-blind reviewed by the Program Committee on
the basis of technical quality, relevance to data mining, originality,
significance, and clarity. Author names and affiliations must not
appear in the submissions, and bibliographic references must be
adjusted to preserve author anonymity. Accepted papers will be
published in the conference proceedings by the IEEE Computer Society
Press.

All manuscripts are submitted as full papers and are reviewed based on
their scientific merit. There is no separate abstract submission
step. There are no separate industrial, application, short paper or
poster tracks.

Manuscripts must be submitted electronically in online submission
system (https://wi-lab.com/cyberchair/2015/icdm15/cbc_index.php). We
do not accept email submissions.

Repeatability
*************

Every effort should be made to enable the code and the datasets (or
their closest publicly available equivalents) and all relevant
parameter specifications available to reviewers and readers so that
the results can be independently replicated. While we cannot expect
*every* dataset used to be made public, it is in the best interest of
the authors to make as many as possible available (in the worst case,
a sampled or an anonymized version). To retain anonymity of
submissions, any such additional material should be anonymized as
well, and be published on an anonymous website (such as DropBox). The
repeatability factor will play an important role in the reviewer's
assessment of the submission.

Best Paper Awards
*****************

Awards will be conferred at the conference on the authors of the best
research paper, the best application paper, and the best student
paper. A selected number of accepted papers will be invited for
possible inclusion, in an expanded and revised form, in the Knowledge
and Information Systems journal published by Springer-Verlag.

Attendance
**********

ICDM is forum for presenting and discussing current research in data
mining. Therefore, at least one author of an accepted paper must
complete a regular conference registration and present the paper in
the conference, in order for the paper to be included in the
proceedings and program.

From icnc-fskd-cfp at hnu.edu.cn  Sun May  3 15:09:17 2015
From: icnc-fskd-cfp at hnu.edu.cn (Prof Li)
Date: Sun, 3 May 2015 23:09:17 +0800
Subject: [Cs] ICNC-FSKD 2015 2nd Round Submissions due 16 May: Submitting to
	IEEE Xplore/EI Compendex/ISI 2015/5/3 23:09:29 vcfr
Message-ID: <20150503230929450703@hnu.edu.cn>

Dear Colleague,
 
We cordially invite you to submit a paper to the upcoming 2015 11th International Conference on Natural Computation (ICNC 2015) and 2015 12th International Conference on Fuzzy Systems and Knowledge Discovery (FSKD 2015), to be jointly held from 15-17 August 2015 in Zhangjiajie, China. The deadline for the 2nd (final) round of submissions is 16 May 2015 (papers already submitted in the previous round should not be re-submitted and will receive review notifications on 15 April). Extended versions of selected best papers will appear in 3 SCI-index ICNC-FSKD special issues of Journal of Intelligent & Fuzzy Systems, International Journal of Pattern Recognition and Artificial Intelligence and International Journal of Parallel Programming.
 
Zhangjiajie is a city in the northwestern part of Hunan province. Nearby is the Wulingyuan Scenic Area, a UNESCO World Heritage Site and an AAAAA (the highest class) scenic area in China. Towering sandstones mesas, dense forests, and deep ravines form the gorgeous and mysterious natural landscape. With many spectacularly-shaped stone pillars, hidden valleys, seas of cloud, majestic waterfalls, wandering streams, clear lakes, and limestone caves, Wulingyuan is a must-see in China. Avatar, James Cameron?s block-buster movie, did much of its filming in these beautiful mountains.  
 
As with the past ICNC-FSKD conferences, all papers in conference proceedings will be submitted to both EI Compendex and ISTP (ISI Proceedings), as well as IEEE Xplore (all previous ICNC-FSKD conferences from 2005 to 2013 have been indexed in Ei Compendex). Extended versions of selected best papers will appear in an ICNC-FSKD special issue of International Journal of Pattern Recognition and Artificial Intelligence, a SCI-index journal. ICNC-FSKD 2015 is technically co-sponsored by the IEEE Circuits and Systems Society (pending).
 
ICNC-FSKD is a premier international forum for scientists and researchers to present the state of the art of data mining and intelligent methods inspired from nature, particularly biological, linguistic, and physical systems, with applications to computers, circuits, systems, control, robotics, communications, and more. This is an exciting and emerging interdisciplinary area in which a wide range of theory and methodologies are being investigated and developed to tackle complex and challenging problems. The registration fee of US-D410 includes proceedings, lunches, dinners, banquet, coffee breaks, and all technical sessions.
 
To promote international participation of researchers from outside the country/region where the conference is held (i.e., China?s mainland), researchers outside of China?s mainland are encouraged to propose invited sessions. An honorarium of US-D400 will be enjoyed by the organizer(s) for each completed (with at least 6 registered papers) invited session. The first author of each paper in an invited session must not be affiliated with an organization in China?s mainland. "(Invited Paper)" may be added below the title of each paper in the invited sessions. Invited session organizers will solicit submissions, conduct reviews and recommend accept/reject decisions on the submitted papers. Invited session organizers will be able to set their own submission and review schedules, as long as a set of recommended papers is determined by 3 June 2015. Each invited session proposal should include: (1) the name, bio, and contact information of each organizer of the invited session; (2) the title and a short synopsis of the invited session. Please send your proposal to icnc-fskd at hnu.edu.cn
 
For more information, visit the conference web page:
 
   http://icnc-fskd.hnu.edu.cn/
 
If you have any questions after visiting the conference web page, please email the secretariat at icnc-fskd at hnu.edu.cn
 
Join us at this major event in beautiful Zhangjiajie !!!
 
Organizing Committee
icnc-fskd at hnu.edu.cn
 
P.S.: Kindly forward to your colleagues and students in your school/department.
 
If you wish to unsubscribe, in which case we apologize, please reply with " unsubscribe  cs at ou.edu " in your email subject. Thanks.
 
 
2015/5/3 23:09:29 ahoic0

Hi, just a reminder that you're receiving this email because you have expressed 
an interest in CSTA. Don't forget to add announcements at csta-hq.org to your address
book so we'll be sure to land in your inbox!
Time is almost up to cast your vote for this year's CSTA elections. It only takes
a few minutes to complete and your vote will make a difference for years to come.
Please check for your email from Election Buddy to get your voice heard!
The 2015 CSTA Board of Directors Elections will close tomorrow, on May 4. In addition
to three open positions on the Board, this year's ballot will contain two proposed
changes to the CSTA Bylaws. Each CSTA member, including institutional members, should
have received an email on April 2 containing a personalized link to the election
 ballot. This email will originate from electionbuddy.com, our election service 
provider, so be sure to look for this email and/or whitelist the sender in your 
spam filter. If your email address has changed recently, notify customerservice at csta-hq.org
[mailto:customerservice at csta-hq.org] with your correct address.
Detailed information on this year's election, including the proposed bylaws changes
and candidate statements, can be found at http://csta.acm.org/About/sub/AboutFiles/2015Election.html
[http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?f=0010VJPUQ9B5WZ_ctFaLQ1RtKtTUf8QuShc3rKIp-JzyCNC_jxT_Qgzds-4cWTitv3AVV7wpZAYFUHME5HY15bdJVrikJP1kbNGYt6ec4q0cP0RICWrT5uEDbPLQ6LLqPn2-DXW6kpd3E0tAbN0HP7d_25brTuIdXi6KOnsey2XGv3ju-rCGrL_57k0vfI18t4dngW1-wrB4Rj1hesmfUUAXyFD_N5WZn27&c=yF-1pgVJoz98UTmN1e2pQRBakgJGu5NVerXVAAtjMJAwOCU5YB8D1g==&ch=1Sc6kp9aKRwVquOt2EccLibBD9BfnHs_Y6tSfzMNk51xnfZ0qAtYiw==]

DURING THE HANDS-ON SCIENCE & RECRUITMENT FAIR
Details about this terrific (free) outreach opportunity may be found below.
[cid:image001.jpg at 01D083FB.074B4DF0]

Additional Information:
There is no registration fee or booth charge--the event is free, but registration is required.  Default presentation space will include a covered/draped 6 ft. table and 2 chairs.  Additional tables/chairs may be requested at the time of registration.  A light breakfast and box lunch will be provided to all registered vendors/volunteers.
You will be reaching students and teachers from all across Oklahoma; approximately 800 participants from 60+ schools are anticipated.  We encourage organizations that plan to host traditional recruitment booths to consider including some sort of interactive, hands-on experience at their table to more fully engage students.  A brief 1-2 minute activity can be a terrific conversation starter!  Also, students get excited about freebies, so (if possible) plan to bring promotional materials, giveaways, etc., to further engage students.  These items should be distributed informally and directly to student from your booth throughout the day.
Follow these steps to secure your booth space and register your attendants:

1.    One person from your group should submit the Booth Registration Form (via the Booth Registration link below) on your organization's behalf.  The deadline to register a booth is Monday, Aug. 31 or when maximum capacity has been reached.

2.    If your organization will be sponsoring two separate booths (i.e. two hands-on science booths or hands-on science plus a recruitment booth), you only need to complete one online form to register both booths.

3.    Everyone who will be attending the conference in support of your booth must individually register via the Vendors/Volunteers<http://www.okepscor.org/calendar/2015wis> link at the very bottom of the conference Webpage at http://www.okepscor.org/calendar/2015wis by Tuesday, Sept. 1.  (You should plan to send a minimum of two people to the conference to host your booth and interact with students.)

[http://www.okepscor.org/sites/default/files/images/booth-vendor-button-lines_1.jpg]<http://www.okepscor.org/2015-women-science-conference-booth-registration-form-organizations>
Register Your Organization?s Booth (Booth Registration Form link):  http://www.okepscor.org/2015-women-science-conference-booth-registration-form-organizations
Register Your Individual Staff Members (Vendors/Volunteers link):  http://www.okepscor.org/calendar/2015wis

From icnc-fskd-cfp at hnu.edu.cn  Mon May 25 16:49:20 2015
From: icnc-fskd-cfp at hnu.edu.cn (Prof Li)
Date: Tue, 26 May 2015 00:49:20 +0800
Subject: [Cs] ICNC-FSKD 2015 Submission open until 28 June: Submitting to
	IEEE Xplore/EI Compendex/ISI 2015/5/26 0:49:29 klyvlhip
Message-ID: <20150526004929842076@hnu.edu.cn>

Dear Colleague,
 
We cordially invite you to submit a paper to the upcoming 2015 11th International Conference on Natural Computation (ICNC 2015) and 2015 12th International Conference on Fuzzy Systems and Knowledge Discovery (FSKD 2015), to be jointly held from 15-17 August 2015 in Zhangjiajie, China. Due to numerous requests, submission will remain open until 28 June 2015. Extended versions of selected best papers will appear in 3 SCI-index ICNC-FSKD special issues of Journal of Intelligent & Fuzzy Systems, International Journal of Pattern Recognition and Artificial Intelligence and International Journal of Parallel Programming.
 
Zhangjiajie is a city in the northwestern part of Hunan province. Nearby is the Wulingyuan Scenic Area, a UNESCO World Heritage Site and an AAAAA (the highest class) scenic area in China. Towering sandstones mesas, dense forests, and deep ravines form the gorgeous and mysterious natural landscape. With many spectacularly-shaped stone pillars, hidden valleys, seas of cloud, majestic waterfalls, wandering streams, clear lakes, and limestone caves, Wulingyuan is a must-see in China. Avatar, James Cameron?s block-buster movie, did much of its filming in these beautiful mountains.  
 
As with the past ICNC-FSKD conferences, all papers in conference proceedings will be submitted to both EI Compendex and ISTP (ISI Proceedings), as well as IEEE Xplore (all previous ICNC-FSKD conferences from 2005 to 2013 have been indexed in Ei Compendex). Extended versions of selected best papers will appear in an ICNC-FSKD special issue of International Journal of Pattern Recognition and Artificial Intelligence, a SCI-index journal. ICNC-FSKD 2015 is technically co-sponsored by the IEEE Circuits and Systems Society (pending).
 
ICNC-FSKD is a premier international forum for scientists and researchers to present the state of the art of data mining and intelligent methods inspired from nature, particularly biological, linguistic, and physical systems, with applications to computers, circuits, systems, control, robotics, communications, and more. This is an exciting and emerging interdisciplinary area in which a wide range of theory and methodologies are being investigated and developed to tackle complex and challenging problems. The registration fee of US-D410 includes proceedings, lunches, dinners, banquet, coffee breaks, and all technical sessions.
 
To promote international participation of researchers from outside the country/region where the conference is held (i.e., China?s mainland), researchers outside of China?s mainland are encouraged to propose invited sessions. An honorarium of US-D400 will be enjoyed by the organizer(s) for each completed (with at least 6 registered papers) invited session. The first author of each paper in an invited session must not be affiliated with an organization in China?s mainland. "(Invited Paper)" may be added below the title of each paper in the invited sessions. Invited session organizers will solicit submissions, conduct reviews and recommend accept/reject decisions on the submitted papers. Invited session organizers will be able to set their own submission and review schedules, as long as a set of recommended papers is determined by 3 June 2015. Each invited session proposal should include: (1) the name, bio, and contact information of each organizer of the invited session; (2) the title and a short synopsis of the invited session. Please send your proposal to icnc-fskd at hnu.edu.cn
 
For more information, visit the conference web page:
 
   http://icnc-fskd.hnu.edu.cn/
 
If you have any questions after visiting the conference web page, please email the secretariat at icnc-fskd at hnu.edu.cn
 
Join us at this major event in beautiful Zhangjiajie !!!
 
Organizing Committee
icnc-fskd at hnu.edu.cn
 
P.S.: Kindly forward to your colleagues and students in your school/department.
 
If you wish to unsubscribe, in which case we apologize, please reply with " unsubscribe  cs at ou.edu " in your email subject. Thanks.

Reminder: Call for Papers and Participation WiPSCE 2015

We invite you to submit a paper, report, or poster for the 10th Workshop in Primary
and Secondary Computing Education (WiPSCE 2015) and join us in London, United Kingdom,
in November, 9-11, 2015.

Submission deadline: Monday June 1st.

Re-submission deadline: Monday June 8th

WiPSCE aims at improving the exchange of research and practice relevant to teaching
and learning in primary and secondary computing education, teacher training, and
 related research.

Special Theme: Computing? How young is too young?

For more information please follow:

Hi, just a reminder that you're receiving this email because you have expressed 
an interest in CSTA. Don't forget to add announcements at csta-hq.org to your address
book so we'll be sure to land in your inbox!
Dear CSTA Members,
CSTA is delighted to announce the results of the 2015-16 CSTA Board of Directors
 election. Listed below are the successful candidates who will be continuing to 
serve on the Board as of July 1, 2015.
Sheena Vaidyanathan
K-8 Representative
Los Altos School District
Los Altos, CA
Stephanie Hoeppner
9-12 Representative
Clermont Northeastern High School
Williamsburg, OH
Alfred Thompson
At-Large Representative
Bishop Guertin High School
Nashua, NH
The proposed Bylaws Changes to Article IV, Section 9 and Article V, Section 4 were
also approved.
Each of these newly-elected Board members will serve for two years. For more information
with regard to these new Board members, please see:
http://csta.acm.org/About/sub/AboutFiles/2015Election.html [http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?f=001Zdz6ck8bCYnBDYbbtei1IFP-fk2wOYEGfDOgZRZkDwMaN5c3HDBsK548H-xsvva1HTSD_vmwQeHw3JU_CENpGxR3sJpCyg_SrJuSGA8uzJ-zKngZlDM7FTUBf4AxyLZIqBugtxn7Ojy5Nb_mytt6mGAiSJvIWUA-m3jIfnXJmSAY_tPHb9_lJuqa-qA0mxaSXjKHjqKOp584m-Q3R0A0Ka_dcehMNTMr&c=abzd0DyidPXIfmfATG1H-jxfQE9uG93vCccn_VeLFHBU-vbZueWO-g==&ch=GuVGZAqrvFaq6-P2Rsu419qt47A9JyHjHea5_nL-svqkM5QmcQ4RcQ==]

EDUCATIONAL ROBOTICS FOR ABSOLUTE BEGINNERS: The Basics of LEGO Robot Programming
~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~

The Rowan University Laboratory for Educational Robotics (RULER Lab) invites you
 to join our free self-paced online courses that teach absolute beginners the fundamentals
of programming LEGO robots. Over 5,000 people have already participated in our LEGO
NXT Robotics Course and we are excited to announce that our new LEGO EV3 Robotics
Course is now open.  Both courses were designed specifically for K-12 teachers, 
but are free and open to anyone who is interested in learning about LEGO NXT robotics
thanks to the support of Google's CS4HS program.

The LEGO NXT and EV3 robots are programmed using block-based visual programming 
languages that (combined with the physicality of a robot and the familiarity that
many people have with LEGO) we hope will be attractive to people who are new to 
programming. Each lesson in these five week courses includes short video clips, 
self test questions, and robot projects. The first week does not require any special
hardware, but after week 1 you'll need a LEGO NXT or EV3 robot and software to complete
all the exercises.

To learn more about both of these courses, please visit http://www.rowan.edu/cs4hs
[http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?f=001nTrGnuwusFNXXXUN3OvZ58g0v5Aom1M8nLlhKK69HjiYnym2UswUrXCweLba-y-nRgC7Rb0mEXM3m6DZWQA7r-7VjYZMOLZPDiX57C85y13AW5AhWmyGSoARP3RZrwchU_k23Rqu8GZVBQW9C17zAeYtzQx37KRYm0DP4EFZBH3qUUhX_bwQ1Q==&c=lBhnboq_VytzHzya0uY-CbHob4bJW-T2pDa6d2jig5oe9jtgpZCeJQ==&ch=zY1E1WTqm_fwbZpH9TPP2vyBEJFshu29P2TAlqMR9gApyPfmujfG9Q==].
If you have additional questions, please contact Jennifer S. Kay, RULER Lab Director,
at kay at rowan.edu [mailto:kay at rowan.edu].

~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~

K-12 Cyber Security Curriculum Info Gathering
~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~

We are collecting and analyzing the current state of K-12 cyber security curriculum
as a task under the National Science Foundation (NSF) and National Security Agency's
(NSA) GenCyber program. If you have any cyber/computer security material in any 
of your school's courses (not limited to computer courses), we would appreciate 
any information you would be willing to provide about it. The material will be integrated
into a report for the NSF and NSA discussing the available curriculum, and areas
 needing expansion in the future.
Contact: Gilbert Peterson ( gilbert.peterson at gmail.com [mailto:gilbert.peterson at gmail.com]
or gilbert.peterson at afit.edu [mailto:gilbert.peterson at afit.edu]).

~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~

New $10,000 Award for CS Students: ACM/CSTA Cutler-Bell Prize in High School Computing
~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~

Dear CSTA Community,

CSTA is pleased to announce a new award aimed at recognizing talented high school
students in computer science. The ACM/CSTA Cutler-Bell Prize in High School Computing
seeks to promote and encourage the field of computer science, as well as to empower
young and aspiring learners to pursue computing challenges outside of the traditional
classroom environment.

Four winners will be selected annually and each will be awarded a $10,000 prize 
and cost of travel to the annual ACM/CSTA Cutler-Bell Prize in High School Computing
Reception where students will demonstrate their programs and discuss their work.
 The prizes will be funded by a $1 million endowment established by David Cutler
 and Gordon Bell.
Eligible applicants for the award will include graduating high school seniors residing
and attending school in the US. Challenges for the award will focus on developing
an artifact that engages modern computing technology and computer science. Judges
will look for submissions that demonstrate ingenuity, complexity, relevancy, originality,
and a desire to further computer science as a discipline.
The application period for the inaugural award [http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?f=001IspVe1wqos88nG8SXHeYdPTFgcH4iyT8IRkVMk0IFYHhyyL0wtgBKUhtEwWUJYLqbBdUPeRkNF3ibfDBJ1LZDC3Q4lQ-_Cnp2QFgyFEzloYN93mPM6VJeRx_8dSZCyUFoII2XN0_Rew3kvwwmFEOOjttQe3UajMECKkJw7mi8aX3xr3uKYEg5exDkiwFlLKfHLz-n7HDVyWfhU_THRGl2ZqMms5pKnbN_UW-3Q9pMOs=&c=B-CVuw8BfxvNwxUKH-096tebKjpvHigu-JH15MIBQFWbfAueSpNCtQ==&ch=2umqKgvNvhoz5gu2_xD1qfFk_ElaStukMmtKlPo_MSjD_z2JhVfQ_Q==]
is scheduled to open August 1, 2015 and close January 1, 2016. The inaugural awards
will be announced in February 2016.
Please share this exciting announcement with your fellow teachers and your students,
and Good Luck!

View the full press release here. [http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?f=001IspVe1wqos88nG8SXHeYdPTFgcH4iyT8IRkVMk0IFYHhyyL0wtgBKUhtEwWUJYLqKSr00coUD2Qa6GHEpJKW3wy367BebYzrkQP1_35vcx2Z_2B-Tt4KPtSXaM8jrPWIeKxwHCXcRXUsj3bJE8LYbWW0bKGJrPDgQg_O48h3hm9mtySHC5ld1Di12bubALPfH88J8nFMD5d2UywRISySgPvNuWGYlJA4fs90Pl3qwpe8-r0BH_z45tU3nc2BC01q&c=B-CVuw8BfxvNwxUKH-096tebKjpvHigu-JH15MIBQFWbfAueSpNCtQ==&ch=2umqKgvNvhoz5gu2_xD1qfFk_ElaStukMmtKlPo_MSjD_z2JhVfQ_Q==]

From icnc-fskd-cfp at hnu.edu.cn  Sat Jun 20 18:04:36 2015
From: icnc-fskd-cfp at hnu.edu.cn (Prof Li)
Date: Sun, 21 Jun 2015 02:04:36 +0800
Subject: [Cs] ICNC-FSKD 2015 Submission open until 28 June: Submitting to
	IEEE Xplore/EI Compendex/ISI 2015/6/21 2:04:44 uek
Message-ID: <20150621020444153056@hnu.edu.cn>

Dear Colleague,
 
We cordially invite you to submit a paper to the upcoming 2015 11th International Conference on Natural Computation (ICNC 2015) and 2015 12th International Conference on Fuzzy Systems and Knowledge Discovery (FSKD 2015), to be jointly held from 15-17 August 2015 in Zhangjiajie, China. Due to numerous requests, submission will remain open until 28 June 2015. Extended versions of selected best papers will appear in4 SCI-index ICNC-FSKD special issues of Journal of Intelligent & Fuzzy Systems, International Journal of Pattern Recognition and Artificial Intelligence, Concurrency and Computation: Practice & Experience, and International Journal of Parallel Programming (65+ papers). 
 
Zhangjiajie is a city in the northwestern part of Hunan province. Nearby is the Wulingyuan Scenic Area, a UNESCO World Heritage Site and an AAAAA (the highest class) scenic area in China. Towering sandstones mesas, dense forests, and deep ravines form the gorgeous and mysterious natural landscape. With many spectacularly-shaped stone pillars, hidden valleys, seas of cloud, majestic waterfalls, wandering streams, clear lakes, and limestone caves, Wulingyuan is a must-see in China. Avatar, James Cameron?s block-buster movie, did much of its filming in these beautiful mountains.  
 
As with the past ICNC-FSKD conferences, all papers in conference proceedings will be submitted to both EI Compendex and ISTP (ISI Proceedings), as well as IEEE Xplore (all previous ICNC-FSKD conferences from 2005 to 2013 have been indexed in Ei Compendex). Extended versions of selected best papers will appear in an ICNC-FSKD special issue of International Journal of Pattern Recognition and Artificial Intelligence, a SCI-index journal. ICNC-FSKD 2015 is technically co-sponsored by the IEEE Circuits and Systems Society (pending).
 
ICNC-FSKD is a premier international forum for scientists and researchers to present the state of the art of data mining and intelligent methods inspired from nature, particularly biological, linguistic, and physical systems, with applications to computers, circuits, systems, control, robotics, communications, and more. This is an exciting and emerging interdisciplinary area in which a wide range of theory and methodologies are being investigated and developed to tackle complex and challenging problems. The registration fee of US-D410 includes proceedings, lunches, dinners, banquet, coffee breaks, and all technical sessions.
 
To promote international participation of researchers from outside the country/region where the conference is held (i.e., China?s mainland), researchers outside of China?s mainland are encouraged to propose invited sessions. An honorarium of US-D400 will be enjoyed by the organizer(s) for each completed (with at least 6 registered papers) invited session. The first author of each paper in an invited session must not be affiliated with an organization in China?s mainland. "(Invited Paper)" may be added below the title of each paper in the invited sessions. Invited session organizers will solicit submissions, conduct reviews and recommend accept/reject decisions on the submitted papers. Invited session organizers will be able to set their own submission and review schedules, as long as a set of recommended papers is determined by 3 June 2015. Each invited session proposal should include: (1) the name, bio, and contact information of each organizer of the invited session; (2) the title and a short synopsis of the invited session. Please send your proposal to icnc-fskd at hnu.edu.cn
 
For more information, visit the conference web page:
 
   http://icnc-fskd.hnu.edu.cn/
 
If you have any questions after visiting the conference web page, please email the secretariat at icnc-fskd at hnu.edu.cn
 
Join us at this major event in beautiful Zhangjiajie !!!
 
Organizing Committee
icnc-fskd at hnu.edu.cn
 
P.S.: Kindly forward to your colleagues and students in your school/department.
 
If you wish to unsubscribe, in which case we apologize, please reply with " unsubscribe  cs at ou.edu " in your email subject. Thanks.
 
 
2015/6/21 2:04:44 t3usd

Call for teachers:

20th Annual Conference on Innovation and Technology in Computer Science Education
~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~

Working Group 5:

A repository for high school computer science questions and visual assessment tools

CALL FOR TEACHERS

The members of the fifth working group at the ACM 20th annual Conference on Innovation
and Technology in Computer Science Education (http://www.iticse2015.mii.vu.lt/ [http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?f=001UcKw-PDlJBwdNO3wfOn7wTGaJpwa8GprhiSS13ciWtW1XQPsQp5ghC1JhnMpM2xVCwBzelJJYe_8zIthhzf_E-B0o7RDYei7LfRpsV2qiJilnFNX5FBsW9kflLDmoVWNl5VDa77vpRj8_vbvbwfS2SP50NihU9rGDskb7dTklPjiFyRYmCO2dQ==&c=lRkqNpSeqt-kyi0MwYnyIrdf4g1g1wsV1RL8xwQrT97BIDG73GofcQ==&ch=vymzEfN4_wBXVxTvIUem_WNDFhgh9MZgClAIItBkeMEreA2kvp8_pA==])
are pleased to invite Computer Science and STEM teachers to participate, as co-designers,
in the activities of the working group.

Further information and a link to an expression of interest form can be found at

https://sites.google.com/site/iticse2015callforteachers/ [http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?f=001UcKw-PDlJBwdNO3wfOn7wTGaJpwa8GprhiSS13ciWtW1XQPsQp5ghC1JhnMpM2xVjaswmzr9k5kD15hojjK06A1k8y3WxSixiyjgDOegVCsrrkCbDgb0_SCb-Bkxh5TW14Ltg46-CE_oEd9Aj1a8dNc7S75nQF30hNoNr4psGHMPJuZtZAi40WELOAsprK9wtOe8DWjjfIGmmQ2AfYpEFXq8vsK-CmAq&c=lRkqNpSeqt-kyi0MwYnyIrdf4g1g1wsV1RL8xwQrT97BIDG73GofcQ==&ch=vymzEfN4_wBXVxTvIUem_WNDFhgh9MZgClAIItBkeMEreA2kvp8_pA==]

Interested participants please fill in the form: http://bit.ly/1eFA2hj [http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?f=001UcKw-PDlJBwdNO3wfOn7wTGaJpwa8GprhiSS13ciWtW1XQPsQp5ghC1JhnMpM2xVdHynKV6Qj8TJ9MT6xUHUrzyGiE46NVoPi6pIglVENc64MqQCUE62abVM76C1LnPLMmcFYmT4XyaS_ojilfV-u69k0KiKbRsPSdQvk0nDrdY=&c=lRkqNpSeqt-kyi0MwYnyIrdf4g1g1wsV1RL8xwQrT97BIDG73GofcQ==&ch=vymzEfN4_wBXVxTvIUem_WNDFhgh9MZgClAIItBkeMEreA2kvp8_pA==].
The deadline for the expression of interest is June 30, 2015. Afterwards, participants
will be requested to provide their set of questions (from a minimum of one) in accordance
with the given format. Questions can be sent to the Working Group until the 30th
 of September. The questions collected by this deadline will be used to finalize
 the first version of the repository. The collection process will be open until 
the 15th of October to allow further refinements to the repository. The call is 
open, but not limited to, computer science, mathematics and science teachers.

Good Morning,

Hope all is well. I'm reaching out to let you know about an exciting new program, the SANS CyberTalent Immersion Academy sponsored by Solutionary Inc. This Academy is an intensive, accelerated training program that provides SANS world-class training and GIAC certifications to quickly and effectively launch careers with Solutionary in cybersecurity.

I'm writing because SANS and Solutionary (a NTT group security company based in Omaha, NE) are seeking high performing, distinguished students in the region that have recently graduated and are looking for employment in cybersecurity. The Academy provides a unique opportunity for them to not only receive high-quality SANS training and GIAC certs, but do so in a way that leads directly to a job with a great regional employer. Will you pass information (collateral materials attached) on to your graduating and recently graduated students about this opportunity?

The period of applications is open NOW until July 27, and enrollment in the Academy will begin on August 3. Please instruct students to contact Raedawn Johnson at RaedawnJohnson at solutionary.com to apply and visit https://www.sans.org/cybertalent/immersion-academy/programs for more information. Please note - while the Academy was launched for transitioning veterans, we are expanding it to accept applications from high-performing students demonstrating excellence in cybersecurity.

Unconscious Bias in Education - Your Insight is Welcomed
~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~

Hi CSTA Community,
Google is looking for educators' insights on the role of unconscious biases in schools.
They've developed a 15-minute survey to learn about educators' perceptions and awareness
about unconscious bias in schools; and access to resources to overcome it.
Want to participate?  Share your feedback by Friday, July 17, 2015. The survey is
confidential--your responses will not be attributed to you and the data will only
be used in aggregate form. Questions can be directed at: ub-edu at google.com
Link to survey here: http://goo.gl/forms/6nLRddAUAw
